  152. With most aquatic fragrances, they don't last long. Voyage, however, is an aquatic that lasts VERY long. Projection is well above average, also. Being a low-class designer too! This exceeded all expectaions. The perfumer is very good, one of the best too, if you care.<br /><br />Now, the notes and actual smell of the fragrance is stunning. This fragrance is pretty linear, but it doesn't matter if its great throughout the whole period. Starting with a very fruity vibe, with some lavenderish-cleanish-fresh smell. It blends down with some soapy notes, with the fruit staying in there strong; I can also get a little musk in there. Overall, its a very sweet scent, and very masculine for a sweet scent too. Great for the younger crowd, but also exceptional for the 30+'s too. Perfect for highschool, college.<br /><br />Its mostly versitle; mostly intended for the spring and summer. But with the amazing longevity, it can even last in the winter. Perfect for signature scents, I would say. And with the price, you really can't get any better.<br /><br />I don't get the Cool Water similarity. They're very different. Cool water isn't sweet. Its fresh and lavenderish. Despite all the marketing, cool water is actually more 'green' than aquatic to me. Voyage is a true aquatic, that lasts amazingly long. Get this instead of Cool Water. You won't regret it.

  170. I have bought quite a few perfumes from Amazon and sometimes from its affiliates. And many a times, I doubted the Authenticity of the perfumes. After buying this one from Amazon direct, my doubts are now confirmed.<br /><br />I have the exact same bottle from a departmental store, it seems in the originals, the shrink-wraps can be opened from the sides as well. In this case(fake), only from the top or bottom (for easy repackage of return items or demos). I learned that from an expert.<br /><br />Second, the sticker on the bottom of the perfume bottle came off very easily and I could not spot any serial number info either. A very good sign. In the originals, the stickers are very difficult to peel off.<br /><br />And most important test is of course the smell. And the very first few sprays, I knew this was a fake. Smelled nothing but alcohol. What ever little smell it had faded in 1-2 hours. The original one from the dept store lasts for a 8-10 hrs if not more.<br /><br />Someone in law enforcement needs to do something about this. This is getting out of hand if companies like Amazon knowingly or unknowingly are doing this. I have now serious doubts about my Bvlgari Aqua and Armani Aqua de Jio as well. Coz when I had tried them on at the local store, I remember they lasting quite long and the ones I actually purchased from Amazon (direct) for half price hardly makes it through the day.<br /><br />Gosh, I am a perfume freak and have bought at least 15-20 diff perfumes for me and my wife in the last 2 years from Amazon and its affiliate alone. How many of these are fakes !?

  576. Short answer: It smells awful. Do not buy it.<br /><br />Long answer: Colognes are personal. They interact with your personal body chemistry and will smell differently for different people and at different times. Where you spray it (side of neck, chest, on clothes, on skin), how much you put on (one spray or 3), when you put it on (after a shower in the morning, after working out, before going out at night). All of these factors will influence how it smells. Not to mention the chance you receive a knock off as opposed to the real product.<br /><br />So, that being said, Nautica Voyage for men did not smell good on me. It did not smell ok on me. It smelled awful. Like someone let a bottle of Windex ferment on a hot beach for a few weeks. Maybe it was me. Maybe it was one of those scents that do not work well with me. Maybe. All I know is that it was unusable. I tried. Really I did. I used it at different times, on different parts of my body and with varying amounts. Nothing helped. It still smelled like gasoline with chemical &#34;beach smell&#34; added in.<br /><br />I ended up contacting the Amazon support center and explaining the situation. They were awesome. I mean, how can something with 100+ reviews that mostly ships directly from Amazon be a knockoff. Well, a week in to owning this, and I'm 90% sure this is not a legit bottle of Nautica Voyage cologne.<br /><br />The first day or two was amazing. The cologne smells extremely fresh and aquatic and lasted all the way through the day without issue. I was actually able to smell it clearly on my shirt at the end of the day. That all changed by the 3rd use. The smell was still good, but seemed not as potent and dissipated drastically about 15 minutes after application, at least compared to how it was the first few times. This morning came as shock. Out of curiosity, I sprayed it on at took a deep whiff. The smell was pure alcohol, a sort of vodka smell, and then only a slight hint of the actual cologne. It's now a few hours later, and I do smell the cologne on my shirt, but it's a fraction of what it should be.<br /><br />Essentially, I think I got what I paid for: a $15 bottle of cologne. It truly does seem that the spray and tube did indeed have the actual cologne in it when I first got it, but the liquid in the bottle has been watered down with some alcohol. I'll continue to use this for work, because in it's preset form, it's extremely subtle and not intrusive. However, I can't wear it for special occasions or nights out. It's nothing more to me than a decent knockoff. It unfortunately is worth it's discounted price and not a penny more. Do yourself a favor, pony up a few more bucks and buy your cologne from a reliable brick and mortar store, lest you run the risk of getting a tampered with bottle like me.

  1404. A &#34;best bang for your buck&#34; fragrance, Nautica Voyage is easily worth the 20 dollars or so that you'd spend to buy a large bottle. The apple, lotus, and mimosa notes blend very nicely to create a perfect casual summer cologne. Voyage goes on a little scratchy at first, but after 15 minutes or so it settles in and creates a beautiful scent trail. It's citrusy, with just enough sweetness to take the edge off, and the right kind of florals to round it out. What I like most about Voyage is that there's this root-beer like fizz in the mix of it all as well. What you ultimately get is an appealing and addictive accord that persists for several hours before settling into a skin scent around the 3 to 5 hour mark. Projection is average. Voyage is appropriate for any age and best suited for Spring and Summer.

  1619. Summertime in a bottle, plain and simple. It is a straight-up fresh aquatic fragrance, but it has some cool twists that others do not have. It has this nice melon/apple note that is a good change-up from the citrus that most summertime aquatic fragrances are centered around. There is a nice salty air scent as well. The longevity is SUPERB for a fresh fragrance that is this cheap; it easily lasts eight+ hours on me. It is not really a suit and tie scent per se, but if you want something relaxing to wear casually, this one is excellent, although you can pull it off at the office well during summertime. It is a little too beachy for wintertime for my tastes, but if you want to smell like the beach all year round, what is wrong with that? Oh yeah, and this one will get you compliments left and right. I have some fragrances that cost six times as much as Nautica Voyage that have not gotten me nearly as many compliments. For the price, you absolutely cannot go wrong, especially for summer. My favorite Nautica fragrance.
